<details class="wp-block-stackable-accordion stk-block-accordion stk-inner-blocks stk-block-content stk-block stk-88977e9 stk-block-background stk-entrance is-style-default text-accordion stk-will-enter" data-block-id="88977e9" data-height="163.0625">

<div class="wp-block-stackable-heading stk-block-heading stk-block-heading--v2 stk-block stk-ed6285d" id="will-i-need-to-anticipate-disruptive-behaviour-or-allow-for-an-adjustment-period-for-my-child-transitioning-between-eyc-and-k-1" data-block-id="ed6285d"><p class="stk-block-heading__text has-text-color">Will I need to anticipate disruptive behaviour or allow for an adjustment period for my child transitioning between EYC and K1?</p></div>



<div class="wp-block-stackable-icon stk-block-icon stk-block stk-87389a3" data-block-id="87389a3"><span class="stk--svg-wrapper"><div class="stk--inner-svg"><svg style="height:0;width:0"><defs><linearGradient id="linear-gradient-87389a3" x1="0" x2="100%" y1="0" y2="0"><stop offset="0%" style="stop-opacity:1;stop-color:var(--linear-gradient-87389-a-3-color-1)"></stop><stop offset="100%" style="stop-opacity:1;stop-color:var(--linear-gradient-87389-a-3-color-2)"></stop></linearGradient></defs></svg><svg data-prefix="fas" data-icon="chevron-down" class="svg-inline--fa fa-chevron-down fa-w-14" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 448 512" aria-hidden="true" width="32" height="32"><path fill="currentColor" d="M207.029 381.476L12.686 187.132c-9.373-9.373-9.373-24.569 0-33.941l22.667-22.667c9.357-9.357 24.522-9.375 33.901-.04L224 284.505l154.745-154.021c9.379-9.335 24.544-9.317 33.901.04l22.667 22.667c9.373 9.373 9.373 24.569 0 33.941L240.971 381.476c-9.373 9.372-24.569 9.372-33.942 0z"></path></svg></div></span></div>

<div class="wp-block-stackable-column stk-block-column stk-column stk-block stk-318adf6 stk-block-accordion__content" data-v="4" data-block-id="318adf6"><div class="stk-column-wrapper stk-block-column__content stk-container stk-318adf6-container stk--no-background stk--no-padding"><div class="stk-block-content stk-inner-blocks stk-318adf6-inner-blocks">
<div class="wp-block-stackable-text stk-block-text stk-block stk-286fddf" data-block-id="286fddf"><p class="stk-block-text__text has-text-color">All the children in EYC will be guaranteed a space in a MOE Kindergarten. To facilitate positive transition experiences, children and their parents will be invited to an orientation session organised at the partner MOE Kindergarten before the start of their K1 year. At the orientation, children will meet with their kindergarten teachers and classmates to introduce them to the new learning environment. Parents are also invited to accompany their children to the MOE Kindergarten on the first two days of Term 1 to help their child get used to the new daily routine.</p></div>
</div></div></div>
</details>

<div class="wp-block-stackable-icon-label stk-block-icon-label stk-block stk-49234bf" data-block-id="49234bf"><div class="stk-row stk-inner-blocks stk-block-content">

<div class="wp-block-stackable-column stk-block-column stk-column stk-block stk-7eebe6b stk-block-accordion__content" data-v="4" data-block-id="7eebe6b"><div class="stk-column-wrapper stk-block-column__content stk-container stk-7eebe6b-container stk--no-background stk--no-padding"><div class="stk-block-content stk-inner-blocks stk-7eebe6b-inner-blocks">
<div class="wp-block-stackable-text stk-block-text stk-block stk-4bb189a" data-block-id="4bb189a"><p class="stk-block-text__text has-text-color">My First Skool (MFS) is collaborating with MOE Kindergarten to provide a continuum of quality and affordable pre-school education for children aged two months to four years through a new model for pre-school services. Under this collaboration, MFS operates an EYC to provide infant care and childcare services. Five and six-year-old children will then continue their Kindergarten 1 (K1) and Kindergarten 2 (K2) programme at a partner MOE Kindergarten. This new model will help to increase the number of quality and affordable pre-school places in Punggol, so as to support the needs of young families in the area.</p></div>
</div></div></div>

<div class="wp-block-stackable-column stk-block-column stk-column stk-block stk-32f8e8a stk-block-accordion__content" data-v="4" data-block-id="32f8e8a"><div class="stk-column-wrapper stk-block-column__content stk-container stk-32f8e8a-container stk--no-background stk--no-padding"><div class="stk-block-content stk-inner-blocks stk-32f8e8a-inner-blocks">
<div class="wp-block-stackable-text stk-block-text stk-block stk-4f39a7e" data-block-id="4f39a7e"><p class="stk-block-text__text has-text-color">All applicants for Singapore Citizen children are eligible for Basic Subsidy. Additional Subsidy is only available to applicants for Singapore Citizen children a) who are working at least 56 hours per month and b) whose gross monthly household income is $12,000 and below or per capita income is $3,000 and below.</p></div>
</div></div></div>
</details>



<details class="wp-block-stackable-accordion stk-block-accordion stk-inner-blocks stk-block-content stk-block stk-7ee6a09 stk-block-background stk-entrance is-style-default text-accordion stk-will-enter" data-block-id="7ee6a09" data-height="103.6875">

<div class="wp-block-stackable-text stk-block-text stk-block stk-8ab76c2" data-block-id="8ab76c2"><p class="stk-block-text__text has-text-color">ECDA provides a number of financial support schemes. <div class="wp-block-stackable-column stk-block-column stk-column stk-block stk-1742014 stk-block-accordion__content" data-v="4" data-block-id="1742014"><div class="stk-column-wrapper stk-block-column__content stk-container stk-1742014-container stk--no-background stk--no-padding"><div class="stk-block-content stk-inner-blocks stk-1742014-inner-blocks">
<div class="wp-block-stackable-text stk-block-text stk-block stk-bae89c6" data-block-id="bae89c6"><p class="stk-block-text__text has-text-color">Established by NTUC First Campus in 2008, the Bright Horizons Fund (BHF) is a charity fund registered as an Institute of Public Character (IPC). The funds are primarily used to provide financial support for pre-school children from low-income families.</p></div>

<div class="wp-block-stackable-column stk-block-column stk-column stk-block stk-bc77bd7" data-v="4" data-block-id="bc77bd7"><div class="stk-column-wrapper stk-block-column__content stk-container stk-bc77bd7-container stk--no-background stk--no-padding"><div class="stk-block-content stk-inner-blocks stk-bc77bd7-inner-blocks">
<div class="wp-block-stackable-heading stk-block-heading stk-block-heading--v2 stk-block stk-8a19dd0 _mPS2id-t" id="faq-level-3" data-block-id="8a19dd0"><h2 class="stk-block-heading__text has-text-color has-text-align-left">Our Approach – Curriculum</h2></div>



<details class="wp-block-stackable-accordion stk-block-accordion stk-inner-blocks stk-block-content stk-block stk-4e208ff stk-block-background stk-entrance is-style-default text-accordion stk-will-enter" data-block-id="4e208ff" data-height="133.375">
<summary class="wp-block-stackable-column stk-block-column stk-column stk-block stk-499ca67 stk--container-small stk-block-accordion__heading" data-v="4" data-block-id="499ca67"><div class="stk-column-wrapper stk-block-column__content stk-container stk-499ca67-container stk--no-background stk--no-padding"><div class="stk-block-content stk-inner-blocks stk-499ca67-inner-blocks">
<div class="wp-block-stackable-icon-label stk-block-icon-label stk-block stk-ff11991" data-block-id="ff11991"><div class="stk-row stk-inner-blocks stk-block-content">
<div class="wp-block-stackable-heading stk-block-heading stk-block-heading--v2 stk-block stk-fad6550" id="why-is-my-first-skool-providing-a-preschool-service-that-caters-only-to-children-aged-0-to-4-years" data-block-id="fad6550"><p class="stk-block-heading__text has-text-color">Why is My First Skool providing a preschool service that caters only to children aged 0 to 4 years?</p></div>



<div class="wp-block-stackable-icon stk-block-icon stk-block stk-56d36d2" data-block-id="56d36d2"><span class="stk--svg-wrapper"><div class="stk--inner-svg"><svg style="height:0;width:0"><defs><linearGradient id="linear-gradient-56d36d2" x1="0" x2="100%" y1="0" y2="0"><stop offset="0%" style="stop-opacity:1;stop-color:var(--linear-gradient-56-d-36-d-2-color-1)"></stop><stop offset="100%" style="stop-opacity:1;stop-color:var(--linear-gradient-56-d-36-d-2-color-2)"></stop></linearGradient></defs></svg><svg data-prefix="fas" data-icon="chevron-down" class="svg-inline--fa fa-chevron-down fa-w-14" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 448 512" aria-hidden="true" width="32" height="32"><path fill="currentColor" d="M207.029 381.476L12.686 187.132c-9.373-9.373-9.373-24.569 0-33.941l22.667-22.667c9.357-9.357 24.522-9.375 33.901-.04L224 284.505l154.745-154.021c9.379-9.335 24.544-9.317 33.901.04l22.667 22.667c9.373 9.373 9.373 24.569 0 33.941L240.971 381.476c-9.373 9.372-24.569 9.372-33.942 0z"></path></svg></div></span></div>
</div></div>
</div></div></summary>



<div class="wp-block-stackable-column stk-block-column stk-column stk-block stk-0bf33f8 stk-block-accordion__content" data-v="4" data-block-id="0bf33f8"><div class="stk-column-wrapper stk-block-column__content stk-container stk-0bf33f8-container stk--no-background stk--no-padding"><div class="stk-block-content stk-inner-blocks stk-0bf33f8-inner-blocks">
<div class="wp-block-stackable-text stk-block-text stk-block stk-94309e5" data-block-id="94309e5"><p class="stk-block-text__text has-text-color">My First Skool (MFS) is partnering with MOE Kindergartens to provide preschool education for children aged between two months and four years. Under this collaboration, MFS operates an EYC to provide infant care and childcare services. Five and six-year-old children will then continue their Kindergarten 1 (K1) and Kindergarten 2 (K2) programme at a partner MOE Kindergarten. This new model will help to increase the number of quality and affordable preschool places in Punggol, so as to support the needs of young families in the area.</p></div>
</div></div></div>
</details>

<div class="wp-block-stackable-heading stk-block-heading stk-block-heading--v2 stk-block stk-789727c" id="why-is-my-first-skool-providing-a-preschool-service-that-caters-only-to-children-aged-0-to-4-years" data-block-id="789727c"><p class="stk-block-heading__text has-text-color">Why is My First Skool providing a preschool service that caters only to children aged 0 to 4 years?</p></div>



<div class="wp-block-stackable-icon stk-block-icon stk-block stk-ae47f70" data-block-id="ae47f70"><span class="stk--svg-wrapper"><div class="stk--inner-svg"><svg style="height:0;width:0"><defs><linearGradient id="linear-gradient-ae47f70" x1="0" x2="100%" y1="0" y2="0"><stop offset="0%" style="stop-opacity:1;stop-color:var(--linear-gradient-ae-47-f-70-color-1)"></stop><stop offset="100%" style="stop-opacity:1;stop-color:var(--linear-gradient-ae-47-f-70-color-2)"></stop></linearGradient></defs></svg><svg data-prefix="fas" data-icon="chevron-down" class="svg-inline--fa fa-chevron-down fa-w-14" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 448 512" aria-hidden="true" width="32" height="32"><path fill="currentColor" d="M207.029 381.476L12.686 187.132c-9.373-9.373-9.373-24.569 0-33.941l22.667-22.667c9.357-9.357 24.522-9.375 33.901-.04L224 284.505l154.745-154.021c9.379-9.335 24.544-9.317 33.901.04l22.667 22.667c9.373 9.373 9.373 24.569 0 33.941L240.971 381.476c-9.373 9.372-24.569 9.372-33.942 0z"></path></svg></div></span></div>

<div class="wp-block-stackable-column stk-block-column stk-column stk-block stk-77d9753 stk-block-accordion__content" data-v="4" data-block-id="77d9753"><div class="stk-column-wrapper stk-block-column__content stk-container stk-77d9753-container stk--no-background stk--no-padding"><div class="stk-block-content stk-inner-blocks stk-77d9753-inner-blocks">
<div class="wp-block-stackable-text stk-block-text stk-block stk-197a54b" data-block-id="197a54b"><p class="stk-block-text__text has-text-color">My First Skool (MFS) is partnering with MOE Kindergartens to provide preschool education for children aged between two months and four years. Under this collaboration, MFS operates an EYC to provide infant care and childcare services. Five and six-year-old children will then continue their Kindergarten 1 (K1) and Kindergarten 2 (K2) programme at a partner MOE Kindergarten. This new model will help to increase the number of quality and affordable preschool places in Punggol, so as to support the needs of young families in the area.</p></div>

<div class="wp-block-stackable-text stk-block-text stk-block stk-20f8d1c" data-block-id="20f8d1c"><p class="stk-block-text__text has-text-color">Mealtimes are an extension to our approach of learning through experiences. The right nutrition is crucial for brain development, and it is never too early to encourage healthy eating habits. Each meal is carefully planned by our food consultant to provide your child with a balanced diet. Most of our preschools are accredited by the Healthy Meals in PreSchools Programme, an initiative by the Health Promotion Board. We strictly follow its guidelines, so you can rest assured that our food is healthy and nutritious for children.</p></div>
